< Review>
We stopped by here while walking to another place for dinner and man I'm so glad we did.  I love street food and this place is a gem! They have everything you can hope for and more.  Various options for your protein and a self serve style of topping which in my opinion is fantastic, you get to create your taco just the way you like it.  They provide an abundance of everything you would want to add as well as giant tubs of delicious sauces.  Everything about this place is perfect, the vibe, the people and obviously the food.  Definitely a must have if you are in the area or actually even if you are not you should drive over!</Review>

The service was above reproach at this beautiful restaurant in Sonora.  We were a part of five and they accommodated us without hesitation.  We felt welcome.  The only reason I am not giving 5 stars is the food although good was not excellent.  It was original. All in all, a pleasant experience.< /Text>
